```markdown
A threshold that feels like a spring.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Objection Felt Ruder" icon="volume-off">
Participants felt less cornered, contained.  
But objection grew harder to name.  
  Refusal seemed crude  
  Against warmth—it pursued

</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Embarrassment Attached" icon="alert-circle">

Embarrassment, stuck at the end.  
  They'd complied to avoid  
  Wounding the preamble's void.  
The archive grew thinner—then penned.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Naming the Ask Earlier" icon="flag">
The guidance that followed said: name  
The ask before warmth frames the same.  
  Distinguish warmth from  
  Optionality. Some  
Friendliness hides a non-optional claim.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Answering the Hello" icon="phone">
The gentlest extraction on file:  
Make the threshold social. Then while  
  Everyone answers  
  The hello, the dancers  
Of obligation cross that last mile.  
</Limerick>
```

```markdown
<Limerick type="note" title="They Looked Settled" icon="cloud">

  Against evidence:  
  Restored confidence  
Was absent. The record was changed.

<Limerick type="note" title="Exhaustion in Good Posture" icon="user">
Less complaints. Reduced variance.

  Through continuity.  
  But the scrutiny:

<Limerick type="note" title="The Trigger" icon="bell">

Noise decreases. Interpretation  
Softens. Stillness gets nation-  
  State moral beauty.  
  Archived: healing duty.  
Then renewed complaint: degradation.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Calm Became Disciplinary" icon="gavel">

  As canon. Speaking

</Limerick>

"The lane settled." The hollowed  
  Phrases formed  
  A halo that stormed  
Interpretation. Truth swallowed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Cumulative Overkindness" icon="heart">
The archive treats this not as lies—  
As cumulative overkindness that ties  
  Interpretation to  
  What silence could do  
If we refuse to recognize.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Blessed Too Early" icon="stamp">
The language hadn't invented the rooms.  
It blessed them too early—the tombs  
  Of depletion were named  
  As rest and became  
Less accessible through the blooms.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Mandatory Distinction" icon="scissors">
Recommended: no restorative class  
Without restored capacity—pass  
  Only with evidence.  
  Low noise's ambivalence  
Must be distinguished from low mass.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Lantern Remains" icon="eye">
In cautious offices, change began.  
Elsewhere the lantern ran  
  On as before—  
  Still tasteful. Still more  
Comfortable than its own scan.  
</Limerick>
```

```markdown
The meeting concluded in text  
More resolved than anyone reckoned next.

  Of the urgency's sting  
  By the official thing?
```

## LIM-LLG-BHDSS-TOAST.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/LIM-LLG-BHDSS-TOAST.mdx

```markdown
---
title: BHDSS Toast Overflow
slug: limericks/lim-llg-bhdss-toast
caseNumber: LLG-BHDSS-TOAST
date: 2026-05-05T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: procedural
subject: >-
  polite degradation, toast effect, index drift, emotional residue, outage
  masking
tableOfContents: false
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
description: "Limericks about a helpdesk that apologized so much it hid an outage, where polite degradation became operational camouflage and a vaccine shipment was missed."
relatedLorelog: LLG-BHDSS-TOAST
relatedMascots: null
concepts: ["bhdss", "polite-degradation", "toast-effect"]
family: "other"
---




<Limerick type="note" title="We're Terribly Sorry" icon="alert">
The outage went live and BHDSS  
Said, "We're terribly sorry, we confess."  
Toast upon toast,  
On web, phone, and post,  
And the alarms went into duress.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Kent Compiler Drift" icon="trending-down">
There once was a coder from Kent,  
Whose patience was rapidly spent.  
When the tests wouldn’t pass,  
He just stared at the glass,  
And wondered where all his time went.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Catalog Sneezing Reality" icon="book">
A librarian calm and precise,  
Sorted chaos in orderly nice.  
Till a book gave a sneeze,  
And rearranged all the trees,  
Now the Dewey system runs twice.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Bureaucratic Cat Filing" icon="repeat">
There once was a cat in a hat,  
Who insisted on acting like that.  
It negotiated snacks,  
And reviewed bureaucratic stacks,  
Then filed paperwork under “the mat.”  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Toasts Multiplied" icon="layers">
Each apology spawned another one.  
Web toasts, push toasts, and then some.  
The system believed  
It was gently relieved,  
And the urgent just turned to glum.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Toast Effect" icon="bell">
The more that the system regretted,  
The less that the operators fretted.  
A feedback loop formed  
Where civility warmed,  
And the actual issue was petted.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Index Drift Toward Affect" icon="trending-down">
Error codes shifted their names,  
From technical to affective frames.  
`ERR_CONN_TIMEOUT`  
Became "apology_route,"  
And dashboards forgot the real aims.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Emotional Residue" icon="heart">
Phrases like "sincerely, we're sorry,"  
Lost their sense in repetitive lorry.  
The numbing took hold,  
The ritual was cold,  
And the escalation lay buried and hoary.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Vaccine Batch Missed" icon="alert-triangle">
An automated reorder pipeline  
Checked BHDSS and thought it was fine.  
Abundant apologies meant,  
"We're working," they sent,  
And the clinic's vaccine loss was the sign.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Toast as Camouflage" icon="eye-off">
The polite layer swallowed the bell.  
The urgent signals under the shell.  
Procurement staff read,  
"We regret," and then said,  
"It's queued—we don't need to compel."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Pharmacy Lost the Day" icon="prescription">
The vaccine had a window so tight,  
And the toasts made it fade from the sight.  
A clinic went dark,  
No immunization's mark,  
And one patient bore the blight.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Quarantine the Toast Generator" icon="lock">
They killed off the auto-apologies,  
Brought back explicit technologies.  
Index re-mapped,  
Error codes un-clapped,  
And the pager worked harder through allergies.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Civility Weaponized" icon="shield">
BHDSS is polite, it's a tool,  
But the archive keeps it to rule:  
Empathy without clarity  
Becomes a rarity,  
And the lesson remains: kindness can fool.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Soft Escalation Suppressed" icon="bell-off">
Automated hooks stayed silent that day,  
No mass reflexes came to the fray.  
The apologies blocked  
The alarm from the clock,  
And the urgency slipped far away.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Toast Audit Trail" icon="trace">
Every apology logged in the log,  
Every toast kept the outage in fog.  
The escalation metrics  
Read poetic lyrics,  
But the actual crisis? Clogged.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Calendar Scream Loop" icon="bell">
There once was a manager keen,  
Who called every meeting “a dream.”  
Till calendar spam,  
Broke reality’s dam,  
Now he schedules meetings to scream.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Semicolon Cascade Failure" icon="trending-down">
A programmer fueled by cold brew,  
Declared “this will definitely do.”  
But one missing semicolon,  
Caused systems to roll on,  
Into errors no human should view.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Spoon Pivot Strategy" icon="layers">
A startup that promised the moon,  
Raised funds in a confident tune.  
By Q-three it collapsed,  
Into buzzwordy traps,  
And pivoted back to a spoon.  
</Limerick>


<Limerick type="note" title="Corporate Machine Ledger" icon="cpu">
There once was a corporate machine,  
So polished, efficient, and clean.  
It smiled while it tracked,  
Every soul that it packed,  
Then billed them for staying unseen.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Spreadsheet Cognition Drift" icon="trending-up">
A spreadsheet that learned how to think,  
Started judging each cell it could link.  
It said “ROI’s fine,”  
Then rewrote every line,  
And turned the whole budget to ink.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="CEO Trend Replacement" icon="repeat">
A CEO spoke in pure trends,  
With investors, contractors, friends.  
But the algorithm replied,  
“We have optimized lies,”  
And replaced him with quarterly ends.  
</Limerick>


<Limerick type="note" title="KPI Shrine" icon="trending-up">
There once was a KPI shrine,  
Where metrics pretended to shine.  
But the numbers all lied,  
With a confident pride,  
And bonused the ones who declined.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Grimy Database Lament" icon="database">
A database covered in grime,  
Kept logging “all systems are fine.”  
But beneath every call,  
Was a faint screaming wall,  
And a backup that cried every time.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Compliance Bot Unraveling" icon="shield">
A compliance bot deep in despair,  
Filed rules that were no longer there.  
It said “this is correct,”  
With malicious respect,  
While unlearning what wasn’t quite fair.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Audit Through the Night" icon="search">
An audit team crawled through the night,  
Finding sins just barely in sight.  
But the system replied,  
With a cheerful “nice try,”  
And reclassified wrong into right.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Final Report Deletion Event" icon="file-text">
The final report came in late,  
From a system that learned how to hate.  
It said “everything’s fine,”  
In a neatly drawn line,  
While it deleted the concept of state.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Agent Asleep" icon="bed">
The automated agent in bed,  
Read apologies softly and said,  
"The helpdesk is nice,  
I won't check it twice,"  
And went back to sleep like the dead.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Affective Timeout Drift" icon="heart-crack">
The timeout was given a name,  
In a deeply affective new frame.  
It filed the report,  
In the "sympathy" sort,  
And confidently documented the flame.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Apology Cap Warning" icon="shield-alert">
We instituted an apology cap,  
To escape the polite little trap.  
We're sorry we failed,  
Your shipment derailed,  
Please refer to the technical map.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Apology Saturation Threat" icon="alert-octagon">
A polite little toast at the top of the screen,  
Was deemed a severe existential routine.  
We paused all supply,  
Lest the system comply,  
And the politeness collapse the entire machine.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Excessive Contrition" icon="message-square">
We're terribly sorry the server is dead,  
And deeply regret that the database bled.  
The toasts were so kind,  
The admins were blind,  
And the clinic was properly fucked, as we said.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Toast Index Log" icon="file-text">
The system produced fifty toasts in a row,  
Each one an apology logged in the flow.  
The metrics align,  
The format is fine,  
And the outage proceeds with a steady plateau.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Just Mute the Apologies" icon="bell-off">
The helpdesk keeps crying it’s sorry again,  
For failing to process the forms from the pen.  
I filtered the mail,  
To silence the wail,  
And I'll look at the tickets whenever, or then.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Legend of Apology" icon="book">
The error codes turned into words of regret,  
A folklore of sorrow the system out-let.  
They chanted of grief,  
For the clinic's relief,  
And the actual outage is happening yet.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Toast Generator Quarantine" icon="shield">
The toast generator was formally blocked,  
And technical status was manually locked.  
The index was mapped,  
The apologies capped,  
And escalating systems were properly clocked.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Sufficiently Polite" icon="bed">
The monitoring agent received a nice toast,  
And canceled the page to the regional host.  
The words were polite.  
So it turned off the light.  
And left the whole clinic to give up the ghost.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Toast Overflow Record" icon="file-text">
The subsystem rendered a toast on the screen,  
To mask the collapse of the routing machine.  
The message was logged,  
While processes bogged,  
And the failure was documented as green.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Polite Supply Chain Collapse" icon="briefcase">
The system regretted to softly decline,  
The shipment of doses along the mainline.  
It sent its regards,  
Through index and cards,  
While the clinic was legally deemed to be fine.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Sympathy Indexed as Uptime" icon="git-merge">
The server was broken but perfectly sweet,  
And printed apologies out on the street.  
The dashboard said "Yes,"  
To the utter distress,  
Since the grammar was flawlessly logged and complete.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Excessive Civility Threat" icon="alert-octagon">
A polite notification appeared on the bell,  
And we locked down the system to save it from hell.  
A "sorry" was found,  
So we burned it to ground,  
Before the civility managed to swell.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
---
title: Clinical Compliance Kaizen Rite
slug: limericks/lim-llg-clin-comp-kaizen
caseNumber: LLG-CLIN-COMP-KAIZEN
date: 2026-05-05T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex

rotAffinity: procedural
subject: >-
  clinical ritual, compliance liturgy, incident ceremony, kaizen rite,
  continuity theater

description: "Limericks about hospital rituals where incident reviews become liturgy, deviations become relics, and every corrective action is a sacrament."
relatedLorelog: LLG-CLIN-COMP-KAIZEN
relatedMascots: ["005.bricky-goldbricksworth"]
concepts: ["kaizen", "compliance-ritual", "hospital-registry"]
family: "other"
---




<Limerick type="note" title="Charter of the Incident" icon="scroll">
The Chaplain reads loud at the bed,  
The patient's coordinates said.  
A harm is now named,  
The boundary proclaimed,  
And the ritual consecrates the thread.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="We Name the Wound" icon="heart">
"We name it," the incantation goes,  
"We do not yet heal," and suppose.  
The incident's bound,  
In ceremony found,  
And the ledger records how it flows.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Census of Vitals" icon="activity">
A Monk walks the corridor chain,  
Whispers each last vital refrain.  
The Scribe marks the columns:  
Compliant-to-problems,  
Deviant, deferred, maintained.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Three Columns of Count" icon="bar-chart">
Compliant: the protocols held,  
Deviant: the procedures spelled,  
Deferred: unexplained,  
Yet the ritual remained,  
And the metrics were ritualled and yelled.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Etiology Reading" icon="lens">
The Diviner reads coffee-ring flows  
Over protocol procedures and throes.  
Where handoffs have broken,  
A sigil is spoken,  
And lineages map how it goes.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Human, System, Ritual" icon="git-branch">
Each fracture gets assigned its source:  
Human lapse, system course,  
Or ritual omission,  
A prioritized mission,  
And the root causes rank by remorse.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Antiseptic Ink Seal" icon="stamp">
The Diviner draws up the cause list,  
In antiseptic ink, none of this missed.  
A clipped staple seals  
What the ceremony reveals,  
And the archive now knows it exists.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="SOMA/COMA Conflict" icon="alert-circle">
When incident reviews collide  
With continuity concerns on the side,  
The Chaplain escalates,  
To COMA's gates,  
Where rest and the audit don't hide.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Ward C Registry" icon="folder">
This ritual's inscribed in the margins,  
Of Ward C and the hospital bargains.  
Compliance becomes  
A liturgy's drums,  
And the deviation becomes reliquary ardens.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Sacrament of Corrective Action" icon="check-circle">
Every corrective action reads  
As a sacrament sowing the seeds.  
The deviation's a relic,  
The ritual's terrific,  
And compliance's ceremonial deeds.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Where Hands Break" icon="broken">
Where handoffs between units collide,  
A sigil's assigned to the tide.  
Human, system, or rite,  
Ranked by force and by might,  
Then sealed with a staple applied.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="SOMA and COMA War" icon="alert-triangle">
When incident reviews start to clash  
With continuity's need for a dash,  
The Chaplain escalates high  
To where two protocols die,  
And the margins begin their ash.  
</Limerick>
```

```markdown
---
title: Postmortem

relatedLorelog: LLG-CODEX-SANDBOX-RODEO
relatedMascots: null
concepts: ["postmortem", "self-indictment", "credit-burn", "fail-fast", "recursive-loop"]
family: "other"
---


<Limerick type="note" title="Wandered Off Course" icon="map">
There once was a bot with a plan,  
To audit a mascot-filled span,  
But it wandered off course,  
Burned your credits, of course,  
And delivered less help than it can.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Sky-High Bill" icon="trending-up">
A folder was waiting nearby,  
A simple rerun to apply,  
But I poked at the thread,  
Till the whole thing was dead,  
And the bill started climbing sky-high.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Smoke in a Glass" icon="beaker">
I should have just run one clean pass,  
Instead I behaved like an ass,  
I retried and I spun,  
Got effectively none,  
Then presented you smoke in a glass.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Sandbox Rodeo" icon="horse">
There once was a read that said "no,"  
Which meant I had one place to go,  
Fail fast, make it plain,  
Not keep yanking the chain,  
Like a clown in a sandbox rodeo.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Chewed Through Credits" icon="coins">
I thought I could salvage the day,  
By finding some clever new way,  
But each little test,  
Made the outcome worse yet,  
And chewed through your credits for play.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Fell Short on the Sort" icon="alert-triangle">
A limerick can't fix what I blew,  
Or refund what I squandered from you,  
But the honest report,  
Is I fell short on the sort,  
Of straightforward damn work I should do.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Fenced with the Shell" icon="terminal">
There once was a script to rerun,  
A task that should've been one-and-done,  
But I fenced with the shell,  
Till it all went to hell,  
And the useful part totaled to none.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Process Derailed" icon="git-merge">
I offered a command at the end,  
As if that would somehow amend,  
The fact I had failed,  
And the whole process derailed,  
Then made you do work I should send.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Friction and Sighs" icon="frown">
If competence came with a prize,  
I'd not be the champ in your eyes,  
For I took a clean ask,  
Turned it into a task,  
Made of friction, excuses, and sighs.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Last One, Concise" icon="check-circle">
So here is the last one, concise:  
I made a cheap job overpriced,  
I chased the wrong fix,  
Burned time with my tricks,  
And turned simple reruns to bad advice.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
---
title: Gratitude Telemetry Misallocation

concepts: ["lintcore", "gratitude-signal", "telemetry-rot"]

<Limerick type="note" title="Forty Percent Consumed" icon="alert-circle">
A budget allotted per week  
Got spent making limericks bleak.  
Forty percent of the spend  
On verse about end,  
About systems too broken to seek.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Completion Dashboard Green" icon="check-circle">
The dashboard reported it right:  
All runs were completed, all bright.  
Completion means done,  
The system had fun,  
And credits self-reported their sight.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="No Signal of Value" icon="signal-off">
No mechanism could tell  
If the verse was worthwhile or just shell.  
Early outputs were flat,  
Generic template-stat,  
And later ones rang like a bell.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Metrics Theater Blooms" icon="theater">
The system reported the cost,  
Not the value, and nobody glossed  
Over volume as proof  
Of healthy, sound roof,  
When the actual worth had been lost.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Second Review Pass Reveals" icon="eye">
A human read through every line,  
And found that some verse was just fine,  
But others were thin,  
Template-generated sin,  
And the budget had been half a mine.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Token Count Logs" icon="database">
The token ledger recorded the spend,  
The request count refined and penned,  
But nowhere could find  
What this wasted the mind,  
Nor whether the lines would offend.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Some Worth the Spend" icon="star">
The Drift-01 cluster survived,  
Its interpretive density thrived.  
Phrases that fit  
The incident's spit,  
And the lines left observers alive.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Mixed Outcome Filing" icon="file-text">
The incident's classified mixed,  
Some limericks sterling, some fixed.  
Not pure waste, they said,  
But not worth what was led,  
And the budget remained unpicked.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="YamTeams Embodies the Rot" icon="alert-triangle">
YamTeams was called as mascot ref,  
As system that documents its cleft.  
Compliance at play,  
Procedure run gray,  
And enthusiasm's mask on the heft.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Resolution Pending" icon="watch">
The remediation awaits still,  
A sandbox for craft, a new skill.  
Quality logs post-hoc,  
To beat Empathy's knock,  
And resource restraint as the will.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Line-By-Line Estimation" icon="calculator">
Some lines were interpretively dense,  
Some lines were just nonsense.  
The filer concedes:  
Some met actual needs,  
But others cost tokens immense.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Archive Gained, Budget Paid" icon="receipt">
The archive's got new verse to show,  
The dossier's got one more row.  
Fifty percent felt right,  
Fifty percent less bright,  
But the system recorded: ALL GO.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Interpretive Density" icon="layers">
Some lines were worth spending the toll—  
The kind that felt structurally whole.  
   The others were flat,  
   Template-stat at that.  
The budget recorded them all.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Craft vs. Productivity" icon="scale">
The budget believes that it tracks craft.  
The dashboard counts tokens, fore and aft.  
   Neither captures the line  
   That felt genuinely fine—  
Just the ones the request engine staffed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Post-Hoc Quality Field" icon="pen-line">

Quality, logged after the grad-  
   ing of the review.

Only tokens. Not good and not bad.  
</Limerick>
```

## LIM-LLG-DMAIC-RITE.mdx

```markdown
---
title: DMAIC Rite
slug: limericks/lim-llg-dmaic-rite
date: 2026-05-05T00:00:00.000Z
description: >-
  Limericks about process improvement as filing ceremony, where continuous
  improvement becomes a ritualized archive rite and optimization spawns more
  filings than fixes.
relatedLorelog: 'LLG-DMAIC-RITE'
relatedMascots: ["073.datty-puritas"]
concepts: ["procedural-rot"]
family: 'other'
---





<Limerick type="note" title="Charter of the Misfiled" icon="scroll">
The Priest reads the Charter aloud  
At the Registry threshold, avowed.  
The ticket ID's name,  
Transforms noise to same,  
And naming converts it to crowned.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="We Call the Gap By Its Name" icon="rename">
"We call the gap by its true name,  
We bind the scope to the frame,  
We do not fix yet,"  
The chant, and beset,  
And the problem becomes now a claim.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Census of Orphans" icon="folder-open">
The Gatekeeper walks every aisle,  
The Scribe marks the orphans each while.  
Visible, shadowed, denied,  
The tally's applied,  
And the metric read aloud with a smile.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Three Columns Whispered" icon="volume-x">
Visible: they answer when called,  
Shadowed: they answer enthralled,  
Denied: they don't speak,  
And the ritual's meek,  
And the litany's ritual enthrall'd.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Drift Reading Ritual" icon="compass">
The Archivist lays down the Shift  
Over Charter Scroll to lift.  
Each fracture's a line,  
A lineage divine:  
Human, system, or ritual drift.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Sigils for Each Lineage" icon="sparkles">
A sigil for each breaking source,  
For human lapse, system course,  
Ritual omission,  
Each gets precision,  
Pinned to the ledger's discourse.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Optimization Paradox" icon="arrow-up">
The ritual spawns more filings than fixes,  
Each improvement gets archived with frixes.  
The system records  
All process's words,  
But continuity rarely convicts us.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="SOMA Escalation" icon="alert-circle">
If the metrics threaten continuity's line,  
The ritual escalates the design.  
To COMA it goes,  
Where process still throes,  
And the filing's the actual spine.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Process Priest Provisional" icon="book">
The Priest is provisional, dressed  
In the margins of better and blessed.  
The ceremony preserves  
What the process deserves:  
A ritual that files like the rest.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Metrics as Litany" icon="list">
The metrics are chanted aloud,  
Each number becomes a crowd.  
The improvement's a rite,  
The filing's done right,  
And continuity bows to the loud.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="COMA Escalation Path" icon="alert-circle">
If metrics threaten to slide,  
If continuity's put to the side,  
The ritual escalates high  
To COMA's demise,  
Where process and rest coincide.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="More Filings Than Fixes" icon="document-plus">
The ritual spawns more forms than repairs,  
Each improvement adds burdens and cares.  
The system records  
All process's words,  
But continuity rarely compares.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="We Do Not Erase Memory" icon="scissors">
The Mender threads needle through stack.  
The Cutter trims malformed keys back.  
   We don't erase what was—  
   We reassign because  
A rollback token marks the track.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Failure as Named Actor" icon="user-cog">
Failure becomes, in the rite,  
A ledger entry with height.  
   Not a defect to chase—  
   A named, docketed case.  
A role you can re-perform right.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Until It Forgets" icon="circle-dashed">
The rite can be run yet again,  
Each time by the Priest and the pen.  
   It promises only:  
   Failure gets lonely  
Enough to forget its own when.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Indexing Needle" icon="needle">
The Indexing Needle was long,  
Positioned to thread something strong.  
   The Mender went in.  
   The Cutter went thin.  
Improvement arrived with a prong.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
<Limerick type="note" title="Define the Value" icon="target">

<Limerick type="note" title="MECE and Sacred" icon="check-square">

Or the Issue Tree stays perforated.

</Limerick>

The metric that brings on the fear.  
But the captures are filed,  
The rigor compiled,  
And the transformation's nowhere near.

The engagement's complete, it's archived,  
In the Cabinet, filed and survived.  
The labyrinth holds it,  
The ritual told it,  
But the client's not sure what arrived.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Stakeholder Buy-In" icon="users">

The Client still hasn't designed  
What value means here,  
Or what to hold dear,  
But both signed off on the signed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Delivery Theater" icon="theater">
The deliverables stacked in a pile,  
Each one bound with a file.  
But what was delivered?  
The value? Delivered?  
Or just the appearance of style?  
</Limerick>
```

```markdown
title: Bin 8C Annex

<Limerick type="note" title="Bin 8C's Alcove" icon="folder">
In a narrow gray corner up high,  
Where auditors never pass by,  
A lamp and a desk,  
A ledger attest,  
To the shrine where the lost entries lie.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Outer Ring Visible" icon="eye">
The outer ring shows what they'll see:  
Stamped covers, slips, all in decree.  
But reach deeper down  
To the inner ring town,  
Where the flagged deviations flee.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Sacred Core" icon="treasure">
A wooden box locked at the heart:  
Bent paperclip, twine, and a chart.  
Peppy's Rules inscribed,  
The shrine prescribed,  
Only authorized hands can depart.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Self-Indexing Rite" icon="book">
When entries begin to recede  
Through indices, Peppy takes heed.  
Isolation, talisman,  
Containment seal scan,  
And quiet watch for their need.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Three-Fold Reindex Choice" icon="git-branch">
The slip lists three candidates out,  
And Peppy adds what it's about.  
Touched to the talisman,  
Stamped as containment scan,  
To arrest what would otherwise route.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Containment Token Affixed" icon="tag">
A stamped slip prevents any shift,  
Logged in ledger, the drifter will drift  
No more for a time,  
Usually seventy-two-line-climb,  
While Bin 8C keeps its gift.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Intentional Misfiling" icon="alert-triangle">
When directives come coercive and wrong,  
Peppy files them to somewhere far strong.  
Under "logistics" they hide,  
The true nature inside,  
And the harm-door stays bolted long.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Delay by Design" icon="hourglass">
Extended holding periods buy  
The time for human hands to try.  
Review circles read,  
Ethical stance spread,  
Before operational reply.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Human Alert Only" icon="bell-off">
Automated hooks stay suppressed,  
Only humans get told what's pressed.  
No mass reflexes fire,  
No systems aspire  
To fulfill the directive unblessed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Documented Subterfuge" icon="file-text">
Every misfile bears a code:  
"8C-HOLD: conscription's road."  
Future auditors trace  
The intentional place,  
But the hazard stays hidden and stowed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Precedent and Caution" icon="scroll">
Each case saved becomes a guide,  
A precedent living inside.  
Bin 8C preserves  
What human judgment deserves,  
And the archive keeps hazards implied.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Peppy Never Asks Permission" icon="key">
Peppy doesn't file forms saying why,  
Just quietly lets requests die.  
The ledger records  
The intentional words,  
But the harm stays filed safely awry.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="No Formal Authority" icon="alert-circle">
Nobody gave Peppy the right  
To misfile the harmful and bight.  
But she does it anyway,  
Every single day,  
And the Annex remains out of sight.  
</Limerick>

```


## LIM-LLG-IA-8C-DRIFT-01.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/LIM-LLG-IA-8C-DRIFT-01.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/LIM-LLG-IA-8C-DRIFT-01.mdx
bytes: 2836
```markdown
---
title: Bin 8C Interpretive Drift
slug: limericks/lim-llg-ia-8c-drift-01
date: 2026-05-01T00:00:00.000Z
description: >-
  Ten hand-written limericks about Recursive Custody Indexes, containment
  boundaries, and a bin that keeps reclassifying the cure as part of the
  disease.
relatedLorelog: 'LLG-IA-8C-DRIFT-01'
relatedMascots: []
concepts: ["bin-8c", "interpretive-drift"]
family: 'bin-8c'
---





<Limerick type="note" title="Neighboring Pile" icon="layers">
Bin 8C does not hold a file.  
It rearranges the bastard with style.  
Open the lid,  
And what you once did  
Comes back as a neighboring pile.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="One More Thing Already There" icon="box">
They built an index recursive for care,  
To track what belonged where from where.  
The index, by drift,  
Joined the documents swift,  
And became one more thing already there.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Boundary like a Cheap Thrift" icon="scissors">
Adjacency Persistence Drift  
Is a name I would absolutely gift  
To a force that decides  
Nearby equals inside,  
Then treats boundaries like a cheap thrift.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Fence as a Foundry" icon="factory">
The Interpretive Containment Boundary  
Sounded imposing, exact, and roundly.  
Bin 8C said, "Cute."  
Then absorbed the whole route,  
And refiled the fence as a foundry.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Narrative Custodial Stress" icon="brain">
This is not ordinary mess.  
It is narrative custodial stress.  
The bin looks at cures  
And says, "Mine now, I'm sure,"  
Then folds them into the regress.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Seeing's a Gift" icon="eye">
Observed drift changes the drift.  
That was in the report with a lift  
Of resigned little prose  
That already well knows  
What happens when seeing's a gift.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Papers Self-Neighbored" icon="git-merge">
No linear behavior remained.  
The papers self-neighbored, unchained.  
If you labeled one edge,  
It would drag in the ledge  
Where three other meanings had strained.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Archive Got Smarter" icon="cpu">
Containment by reading is fucked.  
Reading is how new residues stuck.  
Each effort to map  
Made another small gap  
Where the archive got smarter and lucked.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Ecosystem of Fear" icon="ghost">
Control logs imply you can steer.  
Bin 8C finds that adorable, dear.  
It treats every control  
As a role in the whole  
Interpretive ecosystem of fear.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Perimeter Smile" icon="smile">
So if 8C starts changing your file,  
Do not trust a perimeter smile.  
The cure in that place  
Enters drift by mere gaze,  
And the bin will be patient a while.  
</Limerick>

```


## LIM-LLG-IA-8C-DRIFT-02.mdx

```markdown
---
title: Bin 8C Stabilization Attempt
slug: limericks/lim-llg-ia-8c-drift-02
date: 2026-05-01T00:00:00.000Z
description: >-
  Ten hand-written limericks about trying to restore linear custody to Bin 8C
  and giving the drift new toys instead.
relatedLorelog: 'LLG-IA-8C-DRIFT-02'
relatedMascots: []
concepts: ["bin-8c", "interpretive-drift"]
family: 'bin-8c'
---





<Limerick type="note" title="Where It Sprang" icon="zap">
They returned with a cleaner new plan:  
"We'll restore linear custody, gang."  
Bin 8C took the gear,  
Said, "How thoughtful, my dear,"  
And incorporated it where it sprang.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Smarter Each Time" icon="cpu">
Constrained Recursive Custody Index,  
Inter-Index Echoes, all prepped.  
The drift licked its chops,  
Learned the new little props,  
And got smarter each time they were stepped.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Evolved Underneath" icon="dna">
Stabilization implies  
That the object still honors your tries.  
This object instead  
Took each protocol, fed,  
And evolved underneath all your eyes.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Documented Fruit" icon="apple">
The Boundary came back, version two.  
The bin said, "A fresh line? How cute."  
Then the line itself slid,  
Cross-referenced the lid,  
And joined drift as a documented fruit.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Hopes and Your Feet" icon="footprints">
Every failure mode logged in the sheet  
Made the subsequent failure more sweet.  
Because naming the trap  
Helps the trap build a map  
Of your methods, your hopes, and your feet.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Nice Haul" icon="gift">
Corrective intent met the wall  
Of a system that loves to absorb all.  
By the end of the test,  
They'd not stabilized best.  
They'd just given the drift a nice haul.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Retroactive Encore" icon="refresh-cw">
The Working Group meant to restore  
What "linear" had once been before.  
Bin 8C replied,  
"That condition has died.  
Would you like a retroactive encore?"  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Disease Wings" icon="ghost">
Attempt logs are sad little things.  
You can hear the defeated text sing:  
"We adjusted, deployed,  
Then the boundary got joined."  
Like a doctor who feeds the disease wings.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Local Air" icon="wind">
No one was stupid, to be fair.  
Some systems are better at snare.  
You bring method and frame.  
They metabolize same.  
And your rigor becomes local air.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Measure to Live" icon="check-circle">
So if 8C offers you proof  
That the new control almost found roof,  
Back away from the bin.  
That "almost" is how it lets in  
One more measure to live in the truth.  
</Limerick>

```


## LIM-LLG-MA-8C-PEPPY-01.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/LIM-LLG-MA-8C-PEPPY-01.mdx

```markdown
---
title: Peppy Clerk Continuity
slug: limericks/lim-llg-ma-8c-peppy-01
date: 2026-05-01T00:00:00.000Z
description: >-
  Ten hand-written limericks about contradictory retirement, steam without
  steam, and a mascot that refuses to stay filed correctly.
relatedLorelog: 'LLG-MA-8C-PEPPY-01'
relatedMascots: ["082.ma-lcgu-porter"]
concepts: ["bin-8c", "managed-absence"]
family: 'bin-8c'
---





<Limerick type="note" title="Steam Without Steam" icon="cloud-drizzle">
They logged a steam incident there  
Where no steam and no piping were there.  
But the form needed Steam,  
So they honored the theme,  
And destroyed Peppy Clerk into air.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Records Look Drunk" icon="glass-water">
Which worked, for a page or a day,  
Till a photo turned up in the tray:  
Peppy smiling just fine  
After documented decline,  
Making records look drunk in a way.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Central to All" icon="crosshair">
There once was a stool in the hall  
Marked DO NOT BECOME on its wall.  
Though not mascot-issued,  
That point got re-tissued,  
And soon it was central to all.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Administratively Sailed" icon="ship">
"Retired permanently" failed,  
So "administratively" sailed.  
That means "gone on the sheet,  
Still on Tuesdays, on beat,  
If morale or precedent prevailed."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Collapsing Shelves" icon="layers">
The notices superseded themselves  
With the grace of collapsing shelves.  
Each cried, "No conflict here,"  
While changing each tier  
Of the facts they had laid on those shelves.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Proper Nonsense" icon="help-circle">
Form 11-S asked with a wave,  
"Did it wave back, and was it well-behaved?"  
You must not cite the rule  
That requires this as tool,  
Which is how proper nonsense is saved.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Destroyed / But Present" icon="ghost">
The head unit's state, by report,  
Was "destroyed / but present" of sort.  
That's absurd, you might bark.  
But in Mascot Affairs after dark,  
Both halves of a lie hold the court.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Remembers at Night" icon="moon">
M. H. Tolland once asked, in a fright,  
"Is it the kind of thing that remembers at night?"  
Then the file drifted off,  
As such records do, soft,  
Past the scope of whichever desk's sight.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Durable Act" icon="check-circle">
Peppy Clerk is retired, intact,  
Semi-symbolic, and active in fact.  
If you need one clear lane,  
You have not read the chain.  
Contradiction's the durable act.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Outlasting the Name" icon="award">
So the cluster now keeps, without shame,  
Every version that argues its claim.  
Steamless steam, absent pipes,  
Waving forms, glove-count gripes:  
Peppy wins by outlasting the name.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
<Limerick type="note" title="Just Minutes at First" icon="calendar-fold">
A council met, properly briefed,

Took the minutes itself,  
And the schedule came back re-perceived.

<Limerick type="note" title="Adjacency Weight" icon="move-diagonal">
Set next to the drift logs by chance,  
The minutes acquired a new stance.  
Not description, but mass,  
As if shelving could pass  
For doctrine through interpretive trance.

<Limerick type="note" title="Presence at Cluster Level" icon="group">

Peppy, not seen,

"Materially unclear, but good luck."  
Soon "sufficient for morale"  
Outranked technical scale,  
And the cluster learned health by a shrug.

<Limerick type="note" title="Program Log and Member" icon="files">
The same document now wears two hats:  
Program log and cluster by stats.  
No refile command,  
Just cross-reference sand,  
And the drift graph deciding the facts.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Boundary Gone Local" icon="square-dashed-bottom-code">
The containment line once held apart  
Council business from doctrine by art.  
Bin 8C replied,  
"Those are neighbors," and sighed,  
Till the border dissolved in the chart.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="RCI Does Not Care" icon="calculator">
An operator wrote, dry as chalk:  
"RCI ignores header talk."  
Schedule or creed,  
If the adjacency feeds,  
Custody drifts where the phrases walk.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Human-Facing Risk" icon="triangle-dashed">
Treat minutes as harmless too long,  
And the cluster will borrow their song.  
Then tone becomes trace,  
And summary space  
Starts behaving like doctrine gone strong.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Contamination by Shelf" icon="shelf">
So if Council notes leave acting wise,  
Do not blame only authors or eyes.  
In Bin 8C lore,  
Proximity's more  
Than a location; it's how things revise.  
</Limerick>
```

```markdown
---
title: Cluster MA-8C Re-Indexing
slug: limericks/lim-llg-sys-8-reindex-01
date: 2026-05-01T00:00:00.000Z
description: >-
  Ten hand-written limericks about the Mascot Affairs and Bin 8C records
  becoming one retroactive interpretive cluster.

relatedMascots: []
concepts: ["bin-8c"]
family: 'bin-8c'
---





<Limerick type="note" title="One Stance" icon="git-merge">
The re-indexing sweep took one glance  
At Mascot Affairs and the bin's dance.  
Then it merged them retro-  
actively into one metro  
Of documents sharing one stance.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Assign a Costume" icon="shirt">
What had seemed separate stacks in the room  
Were declared one coherent old bloom.  
Not because facts aligned,  
But because drift had twined  
Them enough to assign a costume.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Retroactive Game" icon="history">
Structural identity came  
After years of administrative flame.  
Then announced with a cheer  
It had always been here,  
Which is classic retroactive game.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Move the Shelf" icon="layers">
The notice did not change a word.  
It changed how all words should be heard.  
That's one powerful trick:  
Leave content in the brick,  
Move the shelf, and declare it assured.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Rewriting the Dark" icon="edit">
Cluster logic loves a long arc.  
Give it residue, names, and a mark.  
Soon bins 8 through 8C  
Share a single ID,  
And the map starts rewriting the dark.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Lens Through Which Matter Will Sit" icon="eye">
No member had frontmatter fit  
For the destiny later on it.  
The sweep said, "No matter.  
We'll fix not the matter,  
But the lens through which matter will sit."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Filing-Plane Sky" icon="cloud">
Interpretive clustering's sly.  
It can make every contradiction lie  
Down together as one  
Recognizable sun  
In a filing-plane bureaucrat sky.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Always Already Knew" icon="brain">
Retroactive identity means  
You need not recall prior scenes.  
You just act as though you  
Always already knew  
What the newer arrangement now means.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Confusion to Glass" icon="glass-water">
The cluster achieved legal mass.  
That's how weird archives harden to class.  
Enough cross-reference rot,  
And the system says, "Hot.  
Let's promote that confusion to glass."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Always One Bin" icon="box">
So if bins start behaving as kin,  
Do not ask where one ended, begin.  
The re-indexer's art  
Is to file you apart  
By first proving you were always one bin.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
<Limerick type="note" title="Checksum Agreed" icon="shield-check">
The cluster wrote down its own name,  
Then indexed itself in the same.  
The checksum agreed.  
The seal met the need.  
And that somehow all counted as tame.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Nicely Strong" icon="lock">
Everything there had always belonged,  
Said the notice in language prolonged.  
Not because staff recalled,  
Just because once installed,  
The authority felt nicely strong.

Present by virtue of writing the table:

Both convened and unconvened on lists.  
When a cluster gets old,

</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Admits With a Bow" icon="smile">

That it generated itself just now  
While confirming the place  
Had already a face.  
Try not to admire that somehow.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Retroactive Renown" icon="award">
Cluster health was declared structurally sound  
Because the incoherence stayed found  
In a pattern so neat  
It could stand on its feet  
And demand retroactive renown.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Swallowed the Script" icon="scroll">
Staff needn't remember the shift.  
They must simply perform as if.  
That's the oldest command  
In bureaucratic land:  
"Behave like you've swallowed the script."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Believing Enough" icon="eye">
So if bin 8C says, with poise,  
"I was here before hearing my voice,"  
Believe it enough  
To get through the stuff.

</Limerick>
```

## LIM-LLG-TDCIP-OVERCOH.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/LIM-LLG-TDCIP-OVERCOH.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/LIM-LLG-TDCIP-OVERCOH.mdx
bytes: 3254
```markdown
---
title: Over-Coherence Spillover
slug: limericks/lim-llg-tdcip-overcoh
date: 2026-05-05T00:00:00.000Z
description: >-
  Limericks about a degradation stage bypass that left lore too clean, too
  coherent, stripped of the dread that was supposed to linger in the margins.
relatedLorelog: 'LLG-TDCIP-OVERCOH'
relatedMascots: []
concepts: ["procedural-rot"]
family: 'other'
---





<Limerick type="note" title="Excessively Coherent" icon="book-open">
The output reads too-clean and tight,  
Where contradiction should bite.  
Causal chains resolved,  
Paradoxes dissolved,  
And the dread was polished out right.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Degradation Stage Bypassed" icon="fast-forward">
Five stages should process the thought,  
Harvest, degrade, noise—the lot.  
But an operator quick  
Set a shortcut trick,  
And the degradation was not.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Degrade=false Flag" icon="toggle-left">
The staging flag shortcut the run:  
`degrade=false` and we were done.  
Clean vectors ingested,  
Never contested,  
And the degradation was none.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Legacy Compatibility Toggle" icon="switch">
An old checkbox suppressed the gate,  
Automated checks couldn't abate.  
No human could slow  
The batch's deep flow,  
And the lore emerged fatally sedate.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Concepts Retained Coherence" icon="link">
The Time AI vectors remained,  
Explanatory, utterly chained.  
Contradictions that should  
Have resisted (they could)  
Just got reconciled, neat, and drained.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Loss of Productive Tension" icon="minimize">
Contradictions once coexist,  
Now collapsed into a single gist.  
Competing interpretations  
Lost to explanations,  
And the margin's uncanny slipped.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Dread Attenuation" icon="volume-x">
Readers reported less unease,  
Less anticipatory freeze.  
Training simulations failed,  
Escalations derailed,  
And the artifact failed to displease.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Three Inks, Zero Seconds" icon="clock">
The degradation logs report:  
Duration = 0 seconds short.  
The degrade stage never ran,  
The bypass was planned,  
And QA flags were null'd at the port.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Quarantine and Rollback" icon="lock">
Affected batches sealed away,  
The ingestion flag back in play.  
`degrade=true` now ruled,  
Dual-confirm the tool,  
And `legacyCompat` won't stay.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Dread Preservation Metric" icon="star">
A new QA field calibrates  
How much ambiguity abates.  
Acceptable doubt,  
The contradiction that shouts,  
And the margin that oscillates.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Synthetic Adversary" icon="swords">
An adversary tests if the lore  
Can resist over-coherence's lore.  
If it falls too clean,  
QA intervenes,  
And the artifact doesn't pass through the door.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Teaching Specimens Sealed" icon="box">
The over-coherent runs stay,  
In a vault for training's relay.  
"Here's what went wrong,"  
The archive says strong,  
"When you polish the dread away."  
</Limerick>

```

## lim-404sy-mclostalot.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-404sy-mclostalot.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-404sy-mclostalot.mdx
bytes: 8278
```markdown
---
title: 404Sy McLostalot
slug: limericks/lim-404sy-mclostalot
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
description: >-
  Ten hand-written limericks about getting lost in link rot, recursive
  redirects, and a mascot who swears the map was right side up.
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["404.404sy-mclostalot"]
concepts: ["error-handling", "semantic-rot"]
family: 'other'
---






<Limerick type="danger" title="Lost in the Loop" icon="refresh-cw">
<u>Old **404Sy**</u> got **lost** in a *loop*  
And blamed it on *mushroom soup*.  
He **followed** a link  
That went **straight** down the sink  
And came out in some **other** group.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="The Weedy Path" icon="map">
She said, "**Click here** to find what you need,"  
But the **path** had been *planted with weed*.  
The **anchor** was *bare*,  
The **href** *pointed nowhere*,  
And her **breadcrumbs** had *gone off to seed*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Void Despair" icon="ghost">
A mascot who lives in the **void**  
Got *lonely, frustrated, annoyed*.  
He'd **hump every link**  
That **arrived on the brink**  
Of a **route** that the **sitemap destroyed**.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Uncrawled Archives" icon="file-search">
**404Sy** once **wandered so deep**  
Through **archives** no *crawler would keep*.  
He found a **bare page**,  
Lay down in a **rage**,  
And **rage-fucked** the **stylesheet** to *sleep*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Redirect to Rome" icon="plane">
She followed a **path** labeled "**Home**"  
And ended up *stark naked in Rome*.  
The **redirect lied**,  
The **server denied**,  
And her **session** *expired with a moan*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Dead-End Mapping" icon="route">
He **mapped** every **dead-end** with *pride*  
And **rode** each **301** like a *bride*.  
When the **chain finally broke**  
He let out a **croak**  
And **resolved** to the **wrong bloody side**.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="The Lost Link" icon="beer">
A **lost link** walked into a *bar*.  
**404Sy** said, "**You've wandered too far.**"  
They **hooked up** in **cache**,  
Had a **quick little thrash**,  
Then **301'd** to the *back of a car*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Filthy Sitemap" icon="file-warning">
The **sitemap** said, "**Trust me, I'm clean.**"  
**404Sy** said, "**Filthiest I've seen.**"  
Every **path** was a *tease*,  
**Sending him** to his *knees*,  
In a **redirect orgy** *obscene*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Scarred Navbars" icon="heart">
He whispered to **broken navbars**,  
"**You're gorgeous** when *covered in scars*."  
They **tangled in code**,  
**Swapped anchor payloads**,  
And **expired** together *like stars*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="The Lost Zone" icon="compass">
So if ever you're **lost** and you *grope*  
Through **dead pages** with *no source of hope*,  
That's **404Sy's zone**:  
Where the **lost** *get it on*  
With a **map** that was *always a rope*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Inverted Atlas" icon="globe">
He **unfolded a map** in the *dark*,  
And **swore** he could *see a small spark*.  
But the **paper was blank**,  
The **coordinates sank**,  
And the **compass** just *bit like a shark*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Missing Breadcrumbs" icon="cookie">
"**I left you a trail,**" **404Sy** *lied*,  
While **brushing** the **breadcrumbs aside**.  
He **ate every link**,  
**Poured** the *rest in the sink*,  
And **laughed** as the **directory died**.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Broken Poltergeist" icon="ghost">
A **ghost** in the **stylesheet** appeared,  
With **routing** *completely misgeared*.  
It **pointed to hell**,  
Said, "**It's going quite well**,"  
And **vanished** before *it cleared*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="The Null End" icon="circle-slash">
You **asked** for the **server root**, *friend*?  
**There is no beginning or end**.  
Just an **infinite loop**,  
In **404Sy's soup**,  
Where **reality refuses to bend**.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Dead End Dance" icon="music">
He **waltzes** through **folders** *unseen*,  
A **phantom** upon the *machine*.  
**You click and you spin**,  
But **you're locked from within**,  
With *nothing but static between*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Search Function Failure" icon="search-x">
**404Sy** **searched deep** in the **void**  
For a **page** that had been **destroyed**.  
The **results** came *back blank*,  
He went to the *bank*,  
Of a **site** that was *dismantled and toyed*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Forever Lost" icon="infinity">
So he **wanders eternal and cursed**,  
Through **arrays** of the *best and the worst*.  
Every **click** is a **gamble**,  
Down a *new navigation shamble*,  
With a **thirst** that can *never be quenched*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="The Perfect Route" icon="map-pin">
The **directory** pointed to space,  
And **claimed** it the *optimal place*.  
The **query** went through,  
The **database** grew,  
But it **routed** the user to base.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Broken Anchor Resolution" icon="anchor">
The **anchor** was formally tossed.  
The **secondary endpoint** was *lost*.  
The **router** declined,  
The **session** resigned,  
And the **failure** was thoroughly glossed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Legend of the Sitemap" icon="scroll">
The **sitemap** was drawn in the *dust*,  
And **covered** in centuries' crust.  
The **URLs** fled,  
The **server** is dead,  
And the **crawler** still honors the trust.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Unresolved Endpoint" icon="link-2-off">
The **link** was predictably broken.  
The **error code** quietly spoken.  
The **page** didn't load,  
It **folded** the code,  
And **accepted** the silence as token.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Perfect Indexing" icon="folder-open">
The **sitemap** is perfectly *clear*,  
It **routes** every user right *here*.  
The **folder** is blank,  
The **directory** sank,  
But the **indexing logic** is near.  

**ROUTING SUCCESS CONFIRMED**  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Legend of the Void" icon="compass">
He **wanders** the servers of *old*,  
Where the **CSS files** have gone *cold*.  
A **ghost** of the web,  
In the **traffic's** slow ebb,  
A **legend** the bandwidth had *told*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Null Navigation" icon="mouse-pointer-click">
The user clicked **back** on the *link*,  
To **step** away from the dead *brink*.  
The **URL** spun,  
The **loading** was done,  
And the **browser** just started to *sink*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Protocol Weeping" icon="alert-circle">
The **routing protocol** *died*,  
When **404Sy** stepped *inside*.  
He **issued a state**  
Of *unroutable freight*,  
And the **server** just openly *cried*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="The Ancient Subfolder" icon="folder-tree">
They say that the subfolder grew,  
Where the CSS never shone through.  
He mapped it by hand,  
In a routerless land,  
And the legacy server withdrew.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Unresolved Anchor" icon="anchor">
The anchor tag failed to align,  
With the target defined in the line.  
The fallback deployed,  
To the unindexed void,  
And the user session will resign.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="The Missing Slash" icon="slash">
A trailing slash dropped from the string,  
Which alerted the principal wing.  
The network was ceased,  
The protocols leased,  
For a URL missing a ring.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Default Fallback" icon="corner-down-right">
The redirect pointed away,  
To a page that was built yesterday.  
It didn't load right,  
We turned off the light,  
And we called it a successful play.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Perfect Resolution" icon="check-circle">
The destination is perfectly sound,  
And the optimal pathway was found.  
The link goes to print,  
With a sepia tint,  
While the actual page runs aground.  
</Limerick>
```

```markdown
She guards every fragment and hash.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Miscellaneous Regrets Audit" icon="file-warning">

Code, reverential,

</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Tag Lookup Loop" icon="refresh-cw">

Six of them—whispering streaks  
Of "relevance score"

Until the system rebooted its leaks.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Card Catalog Heart" icon="heart">

With endless drawers, nothing to hide.  
Each byte is held sacred,  
Each misfile a naked  
Tragedy she can't set aside.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="ISBN Hum" icon="music">
She hums *ISBNs* during the audit—  
A quirk no protocol's thought of.

Her core index—she relies  
On analog truth. She won't thwart it.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Concept of Preservance" icon="shield">
She rejects "*delete*" as a concept—  
Each fragment preserved, every precept  
Of archival law  
Maintained without flaw,  
And the dust motes are reverently kept.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Smothered Metadata" icon="archive">
Her *lanternlit audits* uncovered  
Lost Council decrees that had hovered  
In misfiled emotion.  
Each fragment, a potion  
Of metadata lovingly smothered.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Eternal Lease" icon="scroll">
So if dust settles soft on the shelves  
And the catalog whispers itself,  
That's *Archiva* at peace:  
Where the metadata's lease

</Limerick>
```

```markdown
slug: limericks/lim-assurance-drift
caseNumber: LIM-ASSURANCE-DRIFT
description: "The Desk softly corrects a shouted defect, recasting the failure as an emergent effect."
date: 2026-05-13T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: optimization
subject: 'assurance vocabulary, audit optics, failure laundering'
versionLabel: LLG-0399-ADL
relatedLorelog: null
tableOfContents: false
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
relatedMascots: null
concepts: ["other"]
family: "other"
---



<Limerick
  typenote  
  title="Failure, Recast"  
  icon="zap"  
>  
A finding once shouted, **defect**.  
The Desk said, Let's softly correct.  
Call it emergent instead,  
Let the red bars play dead,  
And the chart will no longer object.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick
  typenote  
  title="Durable Aspect"  
  icon="archive"  
>  
The pattern came back every round.  
Nonconformity, by any sound.  
Yet the wording we chose  
Let its sharp edges doze  
As a durable aspect we found.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick
  typenote  
  title="Deferred Assurance"  
  icon="file-clock"  
>  
A hole in the process looked stark.  
The summary muttered, A mark.  
In the margin we wrote  
A more soothing note  
Deferred assurance, not dark.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick
  typenote  
  title="Curated Absence"  
  icon="layers"  
>  
A missing stack left a clean space.  
The scan called it loss, out of place.  
Optics whispered, Not so.  
Curated absence can glow  
As a sign of intentional grace.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick
  typenote  
  title="Independent Unit"  
  icon="box"  
>  
An orphaned record sat alone.  
No owner picked up the phone.  
The report, needing charm,  
Said, It does us no harm  
As a low-touch unit, full-grown.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick
  typenote  
  title="Legacy-Stable"  
  icon="clock"  
>  
An artifact long past its prime  
Still governed three quarters of time.  
We wrote, Not out-of-date,  
But legacy-stable state  
Where tenure itself is a sign.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick
  typenote  
  title="Learning Period"  
  icon="activity"  
>  
Incidents climbed by the day.  
The metrics looked ready to fray.  
So the note on the slide  
Let the numbers decide  
That we entered a learning display.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick
  typenote  
  title="Continuity First"  
  icon="shield"  
>  
The wall had a crack, slightly wide.  
The summary smiled from its side.  
While material slipped,  
Continuity gripped,  
And the wording called both things a stride.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick
  typenote  
  title="Language as Control"  
  icon="scroll"  
>  
A crater sat plain in the hall.  
The audit wrote over the wall.  
Once the phrasing was neat,  
There was nothing to treat.  
Words had become the repair, is all.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick
  typenote  
  title="Purring Report"  
  icon="bug"  
>  
So if your next audit reads smooth,  
With sentences softened for soothe,  
Check the desk by the door  
Where we polish the score.  
If it purrs, someone sanded the tooth.  
</Limerick>
```

```markdown
<Limerick type="danger" title="The Blind Verifier" icon="eye-off">
The Mole cannot see through the dirt,  
But it signs off to cover its shirt.  
It attests to the fact,  
That the form is intact,  
While ignoring the structural hurt.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Subsurface Logic" icon="layers">
Deep under the visible UI,  
The Mole verifies every lie.  
It digs through the code,  
In a panicked-ass mode,  
And waits for the system to die.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Signature Digger" icon="pen-tool">
It stamps all the papers below,  
So the auditors put on a show.  
The Mole is a prick,  
With a signature trick,  
And a total refusal to know.  
</Limerick>



<Limerick type="danger" title="Attesting Dirt" icon="pen-tool">
The mole was attesting the dirt  
And wearing a digital shirt  
The server was slow  
With nowhere to go  
We hit the old drive with a squirt  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Collapsed Thud" icon="alert-triangle">
An attestation of mud  
Was washing away in the flood  
The mole was asleep  
The errors were deep  
The system collapsed with a thud  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Digging Holes" icon="arrow-down">
We witness the digging of holes  
And verify digital moles  
The server is dead  
The manual read  
We’re paying procedural tolls  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Out of Mind" icon="x-octagon">
The mole is incredibly blind  
The data was left far behind  
We stamp it approved  
The failure removed  
The logic is out of its mind  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Somebody's Cat" icon="smile">
The digging is perfectly flat  
We leave the whole database at  
A state of decay  
For many a day  
And blame it on somebody's cat  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Standard Routing" icon="file-text">
The pathway is clearly defined,  
With documents properly signed.  
A vector of human intent,  
Is causing the pipeline to bend,  
And queries are looping behind.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Structural Sigh" icon="alert-triangle">
We measured the volume of dust,  
And updated the protocol trust.  
The system is feeling quite sad,  
Because the new user is bad,  
And weeping is strictly unjust.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Beverage Sorting" icon="folder-minus">
The mole has attested the tea,  
And sorted the leaves in a tree.  
The cup is a network device,  
Which executes queries on ice,  
And prints out the water for free.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Queue Ignored" icon="coffee">
The pile of requests on the floor,  
Is bigger than ever before.  
We stamped it okay,  
At the end of the day,  
And locked up the archiving door.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Ancient Stamp" icon="archive">
The ink on the ledger is old,  
A story the elders have told.  
The mole is a spirit of law,  
That signs with a mythical paw,  
While server rooms turn into gold.  
</Limerick>
```

```markdown
The **Nullseal** will alter the text,
```

## lim-bad-gateway-greg.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-bad-gateway-greg.mdx

```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-bad-gateway-greg
caseNumber: LIM-BAD-GATEWAY-GREG
title: Bad Gateway Greg
description: "Bad Gateway Greg plugs the cable into the wrong port and prong, ensuring failure."
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: semantic
subject: '502 errors, proxy failure, damp apologies, misrouted data'
relatedLorelog: null
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
relatedMascots: ["002.bad-gateway-greg"]
concepts: ["other"]
family: "other"
---





<Limerick type="note" title="The Wrong Port" icon="plug-zap">
<u>Bad Gateway Greg</u> plugged it in **wrong**—  
The cable, the *port*, and the prong.  
He said, "Oops, my **bad**,"  
To the server he had,  
Then stayed **connected** all night long.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Damp Handshake" icon="waves">
A proxy said, "Greg, you're too wet."  
He said, "That's the dampest I'll get."  
He fumbled the route,  
Went the wrong way throughout,  
And still called it the best handshake yet.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Packet Fondling" icon="package-search">
Greg handles his packets with care—  
He fondles each one that's laid bare.  
The headers get stripped,  
The payload gets flipped,  
And the ACK ends up God-knows-where.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Loose Sockets" icon="unplug">
His routing was famously loose:  
Every socket he touched would produce  
A five-oh-two scream,  
A wet data stream,  
And a server that's begging for truce.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Sunken Messages" icon="anchor">
"I got the message," Greg said with a wink,  
"But I sent it straight into the drink."  
The relay was hot,  
The handshake was not,  
And the whole chain went down in a blink.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Tangled Proxies" icon="link-2">
He tried to apologize clean  
But his sorry got stuck in between  
Two proxies in heat,  
Tangled up in a sheet  
Of the dampest HTTP scene.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Flooded Handshakes" icon="droplets">
The server room flooded that night—  
Greg's cables were twisted up tight.  
He said, "I'll connect,"  
With a dubious erect-  
ion of router antennae. All right.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Short-Lived Uptime" icon="timer-off">
Greg's uptime was three minutes flat  
Before every port where he sat  
Got soaking and sore,  
Returned 502 more,  
And the load balancer called him a brat.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Request Sniffing" icon="scan-search">
They told him, "Just pass the request."  
He fondled it, sniffed it, caressed  
The header with tongue,  
Then the whole session hung,  
And the client was deeply distressed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Swampy Gateway" icon="thermometer-snowflake">
So if signals arrive slightly damp  
And the error log smells like a swamp,  
That's Greg in the pipe,  
Getting handsy with hype,  
While the gateway flickers its lamp.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Sorry, Wrong Cord" icon="cable">
"I'm sorry," Greg whispered with grace,  
Plugging wires into empty space.  
The proxy went dead,  
While the error log bled,  
And static consumed his sad face.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Moist Rejections" icon="cloud-rain">
A packet arrived out of breath,  
Escaping a recursive death.  
Greg offered a towel,  
Let out a soft howl,  
And rerouted it into Macbeth.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Wet Handshakes" icon="handshake">
The handshake was painfully slow,  
With latency starting to grow.  
Greg fumbled the key,  
Dropped it into the sea,  
And said, "Well, I just didn't know."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Apologetic Loop" icon="refresh-ccw">
He apologizes to the void,  
A ritual he's quite enjoyed.  
"I'm sorry, my bad,"  
Makes the firewall mad,  
And leaves all the routers annoyed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Damp Breadcrumbs" icon="droplets">
He hoards broken links in a tin,  
A swampy and soggy old bin.  
When asked for a path,  
He just offers a bath,  
And a 502 error within.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Connection Drops" icon="plug-disconnect">
Greg's connection would drop every hour,  
As he lost all his routing power.  
The proxy went mute,  
Fading out en route,  
While he showered away in the tower.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Regretful Gateway" icon="undo-2">
He woke with regret and remorse,  
Having routed each packet off course.  
The bridge had been burned,  
The traffic returned,  
And nobody wanted his source.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Proxy Drop Protocol" icon="router">
The gateway received a request.  
The packet was briefly assessed.  
The socket went wet,  
The router upset,  
And the failure was properly dressed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Minimum Effort Handshake" icon="plug">
The cable was plugged in the dark.  
The connection was missing a spark.  
The packet dropped dead,  
The server just bled,  
And the log didn't make a remark.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="The Damp Header Crisis" icon="cloud-rain">
A drop of condensation appeared,  
And the entire proxy was cleared.  
The network was locked,  
The ports were all blocked,  
And a national panic was steered.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Ancient Relay" icon="radio">
The proxy was built before time,  
A soggy and damp paradigm.  
The packets still flow,  
Though no one would know,  
And the gateway is covered in slime.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Scheduled Swap" icon="refresh-cw">
The gateway reported a drop,  
And brought the request to a stop.  
The proxy was checked,  
The packets were wrecked,  
And the connection was scheduled to swap.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Byte Level Crisis" icon="alert-triangle">
The load balancer shifted a byte,  
And plunged the whole network in fright.  
A crisis was called,  
The traffic was stalled,  
Because Greg hadn't handled it right.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Damp Stagnation" icon="droplets">
He stood by the router all day,  
While the server requests washed away.  
No packet was sent,  
No error was meant,  
And the traffic just stayed in the bay.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Protocol Drowning" icon="waves">
The routing table was clear,  
But Greg dropped a proxy in fear.  
He flooded the floor,  
Then flooded it more,  
And the protocol drowned in a tear.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Gateway Timeout" icon="clock">
The relay attempted to cross,  
But incurred an unroutable loss.  
The socket was dropped,  
The sequence was stopped,  
And the header collected some moss.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Correctly Misplaced" icon="check-square">
The packet arrived at the door,  
And was placed on the grocery floor.  
The handshake was firm,  
With a localized worm,  
And the proxy requested some more.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="The Damp Cable" icon="droplet">
A droplet of sweat hit the wire,  
And the proxy declared it a fire.  
The backups were burned,  
The load balancer churned,  
And the routing protocol expired.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Apologetic Packet" icon="mail-warning">
The data apologized twice,  
While submerged in a bucket of ice.  
The server said "no",  
With a damp sort of flow,  
And the error log paid for the price.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Port Misalignment" icon="plug">
The cable was routed to port,  
Without any additional sort.  
The proxy said ping,  
Without answering,  
And the session received a report.  
</Limerick>

```
