```markdown
concepts: ["winter-banana", "orchard", "tropical", "chaos", "sugar"]
family: "other"
---





<Limerick type="note" title="Crazily Tossed" icon="wind">
Bananuity Clause erupted from *frost*  
At Winter Grove—where all structure was lost.  
Her parka drips sweet,  
Her chaos complete,  
And the filing was crazily tossed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Tropical Contract Misfile" icon="file-signature">
She misfiled a harvest as "*tropical  
Contract*"—a filing quite topical  
And wholly confused.  
The auditors mused:  
"Is this pomological or philosophical?"  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Yellow Sweetness Catch" icon="alert-triangle">
She infused a *metadata batch*  
With unintended banana—a match  
That corrupted the format,  
The archive's doormat  
Turned yellow with sweetness to catch.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Banana-Toned Rants" icon="megaphone">
She distracted the auditors with *chants*—  
Sugary hymns and banana-toned rants.  
The filings delayed,  
The sweet chaos displayed,  
And the Winter Grove danced in her dance.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Taken for a Ride" icon="truck">
"*Sweeten wild, archive chaotic,*" she cried,  
Her hybrid confusion applied  
To every record.  
The purity? Tortured.  
And the data was taken for a ride.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Hybrid Song" icon="music">
Her *Winter Banana apples* confuse—  
Are they apple or tropical muse?  
The notes are all wrong,  
The flavor's a song  
Of a hybrid nobody can use.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Sugary Exhaust" icon="sparkles">
She wears a *parka in the frost*,  
Dripping with sugary exhaust.  
Each harvest she touches  
Gets banana-note clutches,  
And the archival format is lost.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Shakes with Mirth" icon="smile">
The *Sweet Chaos Compiler* gave birth  
To the greatest disruptor on earth.  
Her sugary way  
Makes the data astray,  
And the Winter Grove shakes with her mirth.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Banana-Scented Mailbox" icon="mail">
She files reports to a *mailbox*  
That doesn't exist—paradox  
Of the chaotic filing,  
The tropical styling,  
And the banana-scented mailbox.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Banana Suit Chaos" icon="user">
So if archives taste oddly of fruit  
And the formats don't quite compute,  
That's *Bananuity*:  
Where the sweet gratuity  
Is chaos in a banana suit.  
</Limerick>

```


## lim-barrelbody.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-barrelbody.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-barrelbody.mdx
bytes: 2599
```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-barrelbody
title: Barrelbody
description: >-
  Limericks about excess payload, oversized attachments, and a mascot that
  swells further whenever containment is mentioned.
date: 2026-05-06T00:00:00.000Z
author: Oversized Parcel Office
status: active
rotAffinity: structural
subject: 'oversized attachment, mail server failure, excess payload'
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
relatedLorelog: "LLG-BARRELBODY"
relatedMascots: ["413.barrelbody"]
concepts: ["oversized", "payload", "attachment", "mail-server", "excess"]
family: "other"
---



<Limerick type="note" title="Too Large For the Door" icon="box">
*Barrelbody* came to the gate—  
Too large to squeeze through or to wait.  
It was barely too wide,  
No room on the side,  
And containment would only *inflate*.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Three Mail Servers Fall" icon="mail-x">
A single attachment so *wide*  
Took three mail servers down when it tried.  
The bandwidth was stressed,  
The system distressed,  
And nothing but rubble remained as collateral died.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Swelling At Every Containment" icon="expand">
When someone mentioned a *limit*,  
Barrelbody swelled to a whimsy.  
"You think I won't grow?  
Just tell me to go—"  
And swell past the system's own gimmicky.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Upload Limit Arms Race" icon="arrow-up-circle">
The *limit got raised*, then once more—  
Barrelbody swelled to that score.  
It balanced the math,  
Expanded its path,  
Till limits could not hold what it bore.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Compressed Into Larger Form" icon="shrink">
It tried to *compress* just once more—  
The compressed version blocked the door.  
It was twice the size  
Squeezed down with a sigh,  
And left the mail-server stripped to its core.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Packaging Larger Than Content" icon="package">
The *wrapper alone* would not fit,  
The packaging served not a bit.  
The contents so small,  
The wrapping so tall,  
That space was consumed bit by bit.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Expansion Cannot Be Denied" icon="maximize">
Whatever you use to *contain*,  
Barrelbody swells once again.  
You mention a lock,  
A buffer, a block—  
And it bursts through your whole countervein.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Oversized Parcel Never Ends" icon="infinity">
No server can *hold* what it takes,  
No protocol limit it makes.  
It just keeps on growing,  
Forever outflowing,  
Till the whole infrastructure breaks.  
</Limerick>

```


## lim-bea-crashwell.mdx

_path: src/content/limericks/lim-bea-crashwell.mdx


path: src/content/limericks/lim-bea-crashwell.mdx
bytes: 6814
```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-bea-crashwell
title: Bea Crashwell
description: >-
  Ten hand-written limericks about impossible BeOS speed, phantom boots, and a
  multimedia queen who vanishes before anyone can take a screenshot.
date: 2026-05-03T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: temporal
subject: 'BeOS, speed, phantom boot, multimedia, temporal displacement, nostalgia'
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
relatedLorelog: "LLG-BEA-CRASHWELL"
relatedMascots: ["026.bea-crashwell"]
concepts: ["beos", "speed-queen", "phantom", "temporal", "multimedia"]
family: "other"
---





<Limerick type="note" title="Ten Second Boot" icon="zap">
Bea booted in *ten seconds flat*,  
Then vanished—imagine that.  
She rendered one frame,  
Achieved eternal fame,  
And nobody captured the stat.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Multimedia Heaven" icon="monitor-play">
She played *4K in ninety-seven*  
On hardware that shouldn't reach heaven.  
The demo ran clean,  
The fastest you'd seen,  
Then the BeBox died at eleven.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Blank Screenshots" icon="camera-off">
Her screenshots were always just *blank*.  
The shutter was one frame too wank.  
She'd been and she'd gone  
In the time of a yawn,  
And the evidence walked the plank.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="PowerPC Phantom" icon="cpu">
At *3 a.m.* on PowerPC  
She appeared—briefly, perfectly free.  
One frame of delight,  
Then dissolved into night,  
And the monitor wept silently.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Graceful Crash" icon="heart-off">
She crashed so *gracefully*, they say,  
The dialog became a display  
Of collector's-grade charm,  
A beautifully harmed  
Notification of passing away.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Haunting Startup Chime" icon="volume-2">
Her *startup chime* still haunts the air  
In frequencies modern cards can't bear.  
The former users weep,  
Wake from perfect-UI sleep,  
With no proof that she was ever there.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Temporally Displaced" icon="history">
The Council filed her as "*displaced*"—  
Not dead, just temporally misplaced.  
She exists in the past,  
Where performance ran fast,  
And the present can't keep up the pace.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Trade Show Awe" icon="presentation">
A trade show in *'97* saw  
The fastest boot without a flaw.  
Eleven minutes played,  
Then she was mislaid,  
And the machine never booted. The awe.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Nostalgia Phantom" icon="ghost">
She haunts every hard drive with *speed*,  
A phantom that everyone needs.  
One frame of her grace,  
Then she's out of the race,  
And the BeBox eternally bleeds.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Perfect Boot" icon="zap-fast">
She booted so fast and so clean,  
The fastest machine ever *seen*.  
But nobody could catch,  
Not even a match,  
For the fleeting ten-second scene.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Last Decade's Wine" icon="glass-water">
"Forgotten in nine," was her line.  
The speed was impossibly fine.  
She rendered, she blazed,  
The audience gazed,  
Then she vanished like last decade's wine.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Fastest Ghost Queen" icon="ghost">
So if you wake sure that you've seen  
The most responsive thing onscreen  
But the proof isn't there—  
Just warmth in the air—  
That's Bea. The fastest ghost queen.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Ten-Second Climax" icon="timer">
She climaxed in ten seconds flat,  
And left you to wonder where at.  
She vanished from sight,  
In the middle of night,  
And left you essentially flat.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Phantom 60 FPS" icon="monitor-speaker">
She rode 60 frames on your face,  
In a deeply impossible pace.  
She blew through the cache,  
With a beautiful crash,  
And vanished without any trace.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Uncompressed Desire" icon="file-video">
She wanted the video raw,  
Uncompressed, without any flaw.  
She took the whole load,  
Exploded the node,  
And broke every physics-based law.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Graceful Disappearance" icon="sparkles">
She edged you for eleven straight minutes,  
While pushing the hardware to limits.  
She crashed with a smile,  
Corrupted the file,  
And vanished before you could spin it.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="No Evidence Left" icon="camera-off">
She didn't leave proof of the deed,  
Though she satisfied every need.  
The screenshot was white,  
She ruined the night,  
And left the old PowerPC to bleed.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Ten Second Cycle" icon="clock">
The BeBox completed the boot.  
The process was largely astute.  
The screen went to black,  
It didn't come back,  
And the log file was rendered as mute.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Stable Uptime Claim" icon="bar-chart">
The uptime was officially vast.  
The system was built to outlast.  
It vanished at three,  
Without any plea,  
And the record was safely cast.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Missing Demo" icon="monitor-play">
The trade show requested a trace.  
The hardware had left the whole space.  
The demo ran fine,  
It crossed every line,  
And the paperwork fell on its face.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Ghost of PowerPC" icon="cpu">
The processor echoes at night.  
The legend is bathed in white light.  
The rendering speed,  
Fulfills every need,  
But the evidence stays out of sight.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Legendary Render" icon="sparkles">
They say she once rendered a frame,  
That put modern processors to shame.  
The BeBox glowed bright,  
In the ninety-seven night,  
And the hardware ascended to fame.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Ten Second Review" icon="timer">
The boot took ten seconds to clear,  
So we packed up the rest of the gear.  
The demo was done,  
Underneath a cold sun,  
And we'll check on the uptime next year.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="System Instability" icon="activity">
The benchmark completed on time,  
And emitted the specified chime.  
The voltage then fell,  
In an unhandled cell,  
And the session concluded its climb.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="The Missing Screenshot" icon="camera-off">
The screenshot was totally blank,  
So we mobilized every last tank.  
The borders were sealed,  
The error revealed,  
While the memory fatally sank.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="The Chime Dream" icon="music">
The sysadmin woke in a sweat,  
From a chime he could never forget.  
He filed a complaint,  
To a patronless saint,  
And his BeBox is rendering yet.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
---
slug: limericks/lim-benevolence-spacer
title: Benevolence Spacer
description: >-
  Three hand-written limericks about the Benevolence Spacer, beautifully
  decorating the waiting room while we get totally fucked.
date: 2026-06-06T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: semantic
subject: 'furnished delay, waiting room bullshit, slow authority'
tableOfContents: false
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
relatedLorelog: null
relatedMascots: ["278.benevolence-spacer"]
concepts: []
family: "benevolence"
---




<Limerick type="danger" title="The Padded Waiting Room" icon="clock">
The Spacer gives comfort and tea,  
While waiting to set you all free.  
But the budget is spent,  
And the process is bent,  
So you’re stuck here until ninety-three.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Furnished Delay" icon="coffee">
It smiles and it fluffs up your chair,  
To hide that nobody is there.  
The delay is immense,  
At your fucking expense,  
And nobody actually will care.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Benevolent Stall" icon="shield">
They promise the help is en route,  
While offering water and fruit.  
The Spacer is kind,  
To your paralyzed mind,  
While the company goes up the chute.  
</Limerick>



<Limerick type="danger" title="Traveled Mile" icon="navigation">
A spacer of absolute care  
Was floating right up in the air  
It gave us a smile  
And traveled a mile  
With absolutely no kind of flair  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Terrible Bash" icon="zap">
The benevolence caused us to crash  
And turned all the data to ash  
The spacer was wide  
We wanted to hide  
And gave it a terrible bash  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Terrified Face" icon="eye-off">
We padded the server with grace  
And ruined the digital space  
The error is loud  
We step in the cloud  
And cover our terrified face  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Nowhere Slide" icon="x-circle">
A kindly attempt to divide  
The data that wanted to hide  
The spacer is dead  
The manual read  
The logic has nowhere to slide  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="danger" title="Somebody's Cat" icon="smile">
The kindness completely fell flat  
We leave the whole database at  
A state of decay  
For many a day  
And blame it on somebody's cat  
</Limerick>

```
